 In an important step towards women's empowerment, the ITBP has succeeded in preparing a girls' hockey team for the first time after two years of continuous work from the extreme Naxal-affected area of chhattisgarh
 mahila diwas (women's Day 2019) par yah ati pichde adivasee bahul kshetra ke liye ek tohfa he
 ITBP started training at its level for 42 tribal girls who were under 17 years of age living in Kanya Ashram of Mardapal in Kondagaon district
 agast 2016 se lekar abhi tak is vidhyalay main pard raheen balikaon, jinke paas khelkud se sambandhit koi gyaan na tha or koi prerana nahin thi, ko prerit kar hockey ke khel main aage badhane ko taiyaar kiya
 Significantly, the girls living in the Mardapala Kanya Ashram are the girls of families directly or indirectly affected by Naxal violence
 inamen se kai bacchiyon ke parivaar atyant garibi kii dasha main jivan yaapan kar rahe hai
 After teaching these girls physical exercises, fitness and the initial nuances of the game, they were gradually introduced on the field of hockey
 itibipi ke hockey coach head consteble surya smith hai jo swayan ek hockey ke achche khilaadi hai
 He and rather the 41st Corps provided these girls with shoes, hockey sticks, jerseys, goal post goalkeeper kits and other important hockey related equipment
 jab in bacchiyon ko hockey ke maidan ke liye taiyaar karnaa shuru kiya gaya tab inhen juute ke feete tak baandhne kii jaankaree nahin thi
 Gradually, they were brought to such a level that now these players are getting a chance to play in the girls' team of Chhattisgarh and the under-17 teams
